const generateUniqueId = async ()=>{
    let attempts = 0;
    while(attempts < 10){
        const candidateId = "EXH-".concat(Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000));
        const q = query(collection(db, "users"), where("studentId", "==", candidateId));
        const snap = await getDocs(q);
        if (snap.empty) {
            return candidateId;
        }
        attempts++;
    }
    return "EXH-".concat(Date.now().toString().slice(-6), "-").concat(Math.floor(Math.random() * 100));
};

    const handleAICoreAction = async function(type, target, parentId) {
        let isMastery = arguments.length > 3 && arguments[3] !== void 0 ? arguments[3] : false, overrideSubject = arguments.length > 4 ? arguments[4] : void 0;
        setAILoadingType(type === "quiz" ? "test" : type);
        setShowAILoading(true);
        const taskId = Math.random().toString(36);
        activeAICoreTaskRef.current = taskId;
        try {
            if (type === "notes") {
                var _parentId_match, _parentId_match1, _parentId_match2;
                const classRaw = parentId === null || parentId === void 0 ? void 0 : (_parentId_match = parentId.match(/classes_class_(\d+)/)) === null || _parentId_match === void 0 ? void 0 : _parentId_match[1];
                const clsName = classRaw ? "Class ".concat(classRaw) : (userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.cls) || "Class 12";
                const subRaw = parentId === null || parentId === void 0 ? void 0 : (_parentId_match1 = parentId.match(/subjects_([a-z0-9_]+?)(?:__|$)/)) === null || _parentId_match1 === void 0 ? void 0 : _parentId_match1[1];
                const subName = overrideSubject || (subRaw ? subRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : "General");
                const chapRaw = parentId === null || parentId === void 0 ? void 0 : (_parentId_match2 = parentId.match(/chapters_([a-z0-9_]+?)(?:__|$)/)) === null || _parentId_match2 === void 0 ? void 0 : _parentId_match2[1];
                const chapName = chapRaw ? chapRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : target;
                // Instant local storage cache check
                if ("object" !== "undefined") {
                    const cacheKey = "achivox_notes_full_".concat(subName || "gen", "_").concat(chapName || "none", "_").concat(target || "none", "_").concat((userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id) || "guest").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, "_");
                    try {
                        const cached = localStorage.getItem(cacheKey);
                        if (cached) {
                            const parsed = JSON.parse(cached);
                            if (parsed && parsed.topics) {
                                setShowAILoading(false);
                                setActiveNotes({
                                    title: target,
                                    chapter: chapName,
                                    subjectContext: subName,
                                    classContext: clsName,
                                    mode: "full",
                                    data: parsed
                                });
                                return;
                            }
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                        console.warn("Local cache check failed:", e);
                    }
                }
                if (!(userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.isSubscribed)) {
                    const { allowed } = await checkAndIncrementUsage(userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id, "Smart Notes", 1, target);
                    if (!allowed) {
                        setShowAILoading(false);
                        setShowSubscriptionModal(true);
                        return;
                    }
                }
                const notes = await fetchChapterNotes(target, userData, "dual", subName, chapName);
                if (activeAICoreTaskRef.current !== taskId) return; // Task was cancelled
                if (notes) {
                    setActiveNotes({
                        title: target,
                        chapter: chapName,
                        subjectContext: subName,
                        classContext: clsName,
                        data: notes // Pass fetched data
                    });
                    trackTopicOpen({
                        topicId: target.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, "-"),
                        topicName: target,
                        subject: subName,
                        chapter: chapName,
                        cls: clsName,
                        board: (userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.board) || "CBSE"
                    });
                }
            } else if (type === "test" || type === "quiz") {
                // Dashboard Analysis for Test
                const weakAreas = getWeakAreas();
                let finalTarget = target;
                let subjectContext = "";
                if (target === "Daily Challenge" || !target) {
                    if (weakAreas.length > 0) {
                        finalTarget = weakAreas[0].topic;
                        subjectContext = weakAreas[0].subject;
                    } else {
                        finalTarget = "General Science & Logic"; // Default fallback
                    }
                } else if (parentId) {
                    // Check if parentId is actually a subject name (from MasteryRoadmap)
                    if (!parentId.includes("_")) {
                        subjectContext = parentId;
                    } else {
                        var _parentId_match3;
                        const subRaw = parentId === null || parentId === void 0 ? void 0 : (_parentId_match3 = parentId.match(/subjects_([a-z0-9_]+?)(?:__|$)/)) === null || _parentId_match3 === void 0 ? void 0 : _parentId_match3[1];
                        subjectContext = subRaw ? subRaw.split("_").map((w)=>w.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + w.slice(1)).join(" ") : "General";
                    }
                }
                const questions = await fetchQuestions("full", finalTarget, userData, subjectContext);
                if (activeAICoreTaskRef.current !== taskId) return; // Task was cancelled
                if (questions && questions.length > 0) {
                    setActiveTest({
                        title: finalTarget,
                        subTitle: subjectContext ? "Context: ".concat(subjectContext) : "Practice Test",
                        questions,
                        isMastery,
                        subject: subjectContext || "General",
                        mode: mode
                    });
                } else {
                    alert("AI core was unable to generate questions for this specific topic. Please try a different topic or board.");
                }
            }
        } catch (err) {
            console.error("AI Action Error:", err);
            alert("AI Neural Core connection timeout. Please check your network.");
        } finally{
            setShowAILoading(false);
        }
    };

    // Real-time dynamic performance analyzer for Glowing recommended prep cards
    const getGlowRecommendations = useCallback(()=>{
        const recommends = {
            revisionVault: false,
            flashcards: false,
            timetable: false,
            quickStudy: false,
            battle: false,
            scanSolve: false,
            roadmap: false
        };
        if (!userData) return recommends;
        const totalSolved = userData.totalSolved || 0;
        const correctAnswers = userData.correctAnswers || 0;
        const accuracy = totalSolved > 0 ? correctAnswers / totalSolved * 100 : 100;
        const attempts = userData.attempts || [];
        // 1. Low accuracy (< 70%) or high attempts with failures -> review mistakes
        if (accuracy < 70 || attempts.length > 0 && attempts.some((a)=>a.score < 60)) {
            recommends.revisionVault = true;
            recommends.flashcards = true;
        }
        // 2. Active but weak spots -> Skill roadmap
        if (totalSolved > 15 && accuracy < 85) {
            recommends.roadmap = true;
        }
        // 3. Low study engagement -> AI Timetable Planner
        if ((userData.streak || 0) === 0 || (userData.points || 0) < 1500) {
            recommends.timetable = true;
        }
        // 4. Brand new user -> Quick Study Swipe Cards & Battle Quiz
        if (totalSolved < 5) {
            recommends.quickStudy = true;
            recommends.battle = true;
        }
        // 5. Hard doubts solver -> Scan Camera
        if (attempts.length > 8) {
            recommends.scanSolve = true;
        }
        return recommends;

                                        children: /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)(chevron_right/* default */.Z, {
                                            className: "w-6 h-6"
                                        })
                                    })
                                ]
                            }, item.id);
                        })
                    }, path.map((p)=>p.id).join("-") + searchQuery)
                })
            })
        ]
    });
}

                    /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsxs)("div", {
                        className: "flex items-center gap-3",
                        children: [
                            /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)("div", {
                                className: "w-6 h-6 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center ".concat(color),

                            /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)("span", {

                                children: title
                            }),
                            badge && /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)("span", {
                                className: "bg-primary/10 text-primary text-[9px] font-black px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full uppercase tracking-wider",
                                children: badge
                            })
                        ]
                    }),
                    /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)(proxy/* motion */.E.div, {
                        animate: {
                            rotate: open ? 180 : 0
                        },
                        transition: {
                            duration: 0.2
                        },
                        children: /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)(chevron_down/* default */.Z, {
                            className: "w-6 h-6 text-slate-400"
                        })
                    })
                ]
            }),
            /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)(AnimatePresence/* AnimatePresence */.M, {
                initial: false,
                children: (open || forceOpen) && /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)(proxy/* motion */.E.div, {
                    initial: {
                        height: 0,
                        opacity: 0
                    },
                    animate: {
                        height: "auto",
                        opacity: 1
                    },
                    exit: {
                        height: 0,
                        opacity: 0
                    },
                    transition: {
                        duration: 0.25
                    },
                    className: "overflow-hidden",
                    children: /*#__PURE__*/ (0,jsx_runtime.jsx)("div", {
                        className: "px-4 pb-4 pt-1 border-t border-border/50",

                    })
                })
            })
        ]
    });
}
function SmartNotesViewer(param) {

                }
            } catch (e) {}
        }
        return null;
    });
    const [loading, setLoading] = (0,react.useState)(()=>{
        if (initialData) return false;
        if (true) {

                const localKey = "achivox_notes_".concat(mode, "_").concat(subjectContext || "gen", "_").concat(chapterName || "none", "_").concat(title || "none", "_").concat((userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id) || "guest").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, "_");

            } catch (e) {}
        }
        return true;
    });
    const [progress, setProgress] = (0,react.useState)(0);
    const [lang, setLang] = (0,react.useState)("dual");
    const [showSubModal, setShowSubModal] = (0,react.useState)(false);
    const [usageRemaining, setUsageRemaining] = (0,react.useState)(null);
    const [updateError, setUpdateError] = (0,react.useState)("");
    const [isUpdating, setIsUpdating] = (0,react.useState)(false);
    const [isExporting, setIsExporting] = (0,react.useState)(false);
    const scrollRef = (0,react.useRef)(null);
    const fetchIdRef = (0,react.useRef)(null);
    const displayBoard = (notesData === null || notesData === void 0 ? void 0 : (_notesData_topicMeta = notesData.topicMeta) === null || _notesData_topicMeta === void 0 ? void 0 : _notesData_topicMeta.board) || (userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.board) || "CBSE";
    const displayClass = classContext || (notesData === null || notesData === void 0 ? void 0 : (_notesData_topicMeta1 = notesData.topicMeta) === null || _notesData_topicMeta1 === void 0 ? void 0 : _notesData_topicMeta1.class) || (userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.cls) || "10th";
    const displaySubject = subjectContext || (notesData === null || notesData === void 0 ? void 0 : (_notesData_topicMeta2 = notesData.topicMeta) === null || _notesData_topicMeta2 === void 0 ? void 0 : _notesData_topicMeta2.subject) || "General";
    const displayTopic = (notesData === null || notesData === void 0 ? void 0 : (_notesData_topicMeta3 = notesData.topicMeta) === null || _notesData_topicMeta3 === void 0 ? void 0 : _notesData_topicMeta3.topic) || chapterName || title;
    // Automatic localStorage caching whenever notesData updates (e.g. from parent initialData or direct fetch)
    (0,react.useEffect)(()=>{
        if (notesData) {
            const localKey = "achivox_notes_".concat(mode, "_").concat(subjectContext || "gen", "_").concat(chapterName || "none", "_").concat(title || "none", "_").concat((userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id) || "guest").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, "_");
            try {
                localStorage.setItem(localKey, JSON.stringify(notesData));
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn("Failed to write notes data to local storage cache:", e);
            }
        }
    }, [
        notesData,
        mode,
        subjectContext,
        chapterName,
        title,
        userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id
    ]);
    (0,react.useEffect)(()=>{
        var _notesData_topicMeta, _notesData_topicMeta1;
        // Skip fetching if we already have data from initialData
        if (notesData && (((_notesData_topicMeta = notesData.topicMeta) === null || _notesData_topicMeta === void 0 ? void 0 : _notesData_topicMeta.topic) === chapterName || ((_notesData_topicMeta1 = notesData.topicMeta) === null || _notesData_topicMeta1 === void 0 ? void 0 : _notesData_topicMeta1.topic) === title)) {
            setLoading(false);
            return;
        }
        const loadNotes = async ()=>{
            const currentFetchId = Date.now().toString();
            fetchIdRef.current = currentFetchId;
            const localKey = "achivox_notes_".concat(mode, "_").concat(subjectContext || "gen", "_").concat(chapterName || "none", "_").concat(title || "none", "_").concat((userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id) || "guest").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, "_");
            const localCache = localStorage.getItem(localKey);
            if (localCache) {
                try {
                    const parsed = JSON.parse(localCache);
                    if (parsed && parsed.topics) {
                        setNotesData(parsed);
                        setLoading(false);
                        return;
                    }
                } catch (e) {}
            }
            const startTime = Date.now();
            try {
                setLoading(true);
                // Usage Check for Free Users
                if (!isSubscribed) {
                    const { allowed, remaining } = await (0,analytics/* checkAndIncrementUsage */.TJ)(userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id, "Smart Notes", 1, title); // 1 note per day
                    setUsageRemaining(remaining);
                    if (!allowed) {
                        setShowSubModal(true);
                        setLoading(false);
                        return;
                    }
                }
                const data = await (0,content/* fetchChapterNotes */.oG)(title, userData, lang, subjectContext, chapterName, false, mode);
                if (fetchIdRef.current !== currentFetchId) return; // Discard stale response
                if (data) {
                    setNotesData(data);
                    try {
                        localStorage.setItem(localKey, JSON.stringify(data));
                    } catch (e) {}
                    (0,analytics/* logFeatureUsage */.z7)("Smart Notes", "success", Date.now() - startTime, userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id);
                } else {
                    throw new Error("Neural Core API returned empty data. Check system logs.");
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error("Notes Loading Error:", error);
                setUpdateError(error.message);
                (0,analytics/* logFeatureUsage */.z7)("Smart Notes", "failed", Date.now() - startTime, userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id);
            } finally{
                setLoading(false);
            }
        };
        if (chapterName || title) loadNotes();
    }, [
        chapterName,
        title,
        userData,
        lang,
        subjectContext,
        mode
    ]);
    const getRegenerateStatus = ()=>{
        if (!(notesData === null || notesData === void 0 ? void 0 : notesData.createdAt)) return {
            canUpdate: true,
            daysLeft: 0
        };
        const oldMillis = typeof notesData.createdAt.toMillis === "function" ? notesData.createdAt.toMillis() : typeof notesData.createdAt === "number" ? notesData.createdAt : Date.now();
        const ageInDays = (Date.now() - oldMillis) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24);
        const requiredDays = isSubscribed ? 7 : 30;
        if (ageInDays >= requiredDays) {
            return {
                canUpdate: true,
                daysLeft: 0
            };
        }
        return {
            canUpdate: false,
            daysLeft: Math.ceil(requiredDays - ageInDays)
        };
    };
    const regenStatus = getRegenerateStatus();
    const handleUpdateNotes = async ()=>{
        setIsUpdating(true);
        try {
            const data = await (0,content/* fetchChapterNotes */.oG)(title, userData, lang, subjectContext, chapterName, true, mode);
            if (data) {

                const localKey = "achivox_notes_".concat(mode, "_").concat(subjectContext || "gen", "_").concat(chapterName || "none", "_").concat(title || "none", "_").concat((userData === null || userData === void 0 ? void 0 : userData.id) || "guest").replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, "_");
                try {
                    localStorage.setItem(localKey, JSON.stringify(data));
                } catch (e) {}
                alert("Ō£ģ Smart Notes updated successfully with your latest performance!");
            }
        } catch (e) {
            var _e_message;
            console.error(e);
            if ((_e_message = e.message) === null || _e_message === void 0 ? void 0 : _e_message.startsWith("REGENERATE_LOCK:")) {
                const remaining = e.message.split(":")[1];
                alert("\uD83D\uDD12 Regeneration limit active! You can regenerate notes for this topic after ".concat(remaining, " day").concat(Number(remaining) > 1 ? "s" : "", "."));
            } else {
                alert("Could not update notes at this time.");
            }
        } finally{
            setIsUpdating(false);
        }
    };
    (0,react.useEffect)(()=>{
        const handleBack = (e)=>{
            if (showSubModal) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                setShowSubModal(false);
            }
        };
        window.addEventListener("hardwareBackPress", handleBack, {
            capture: true
        });
        return ()=>{
            try {
                window.removeEventListener("hardwareBackPress", handleBack, {
                    capture: true
                });
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn("Event listener cleanup error:", e);
            }
        };
    }, [
        showSubModal
    ]);
    const handleScroll = ()=>{
        if (scrollRef.current) {
            const { scrollTop, scrollHeight, clientHeight } = scrollRef.current;
            const totalScroll = scrollHeight - clientHeight;
            setProgress(scrollTop / totalScroll * 100);
        }
    };
    const handleDownload = async ()=>{
        try {
            var _window_Capacitor_isNativePlatform, _window_Capacitor;

            // ŌöĆŌöĆ Import html2pdf ŌöĆŌöĆ

            try {
                html2pdfLib = (await Promise.all(/* import() */[__webpack_require__.e(3632), __webpack_require__.e(7337)]).then(__webpack_require__.t.bind(__webpack_require__, 57127, 23))).default;
            } catch (e) {

            if (!html2pdfLib) {

            }
            const opt = {
                margin: [
                    10,
                    10,
                    20,
                    10
                ],
                filename: safeFilename,
                image: {
                    type: "jpeg",
                    quality: 0.92
                },

                    logging: false,

                },

                    ]

            };
            // ­¤Ä© Add print-mode class

            if (pdfSection) pdfSection.classList.remove("hidden");
            let pdfBlob;
            try {
                // Build the PDF and get it as Blob ŌĆö correct chain using .outputPdf('blob')
                pdfBlob = await html2pdfLib().set(opt).from(element).toPdf().get("pdf").then((pdf)=>{
                    try {
                        const totalPages = pdf.internal.getNumberOfPages();
                        const pageWidth = pdf.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
                        const pageHeight = pdf.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
                        for(let i = 1; i <= totalPages; i++){
                            pdf.setPage(i);
                            // Watermark
                            pdf.setFontSize(38);
                            pdf.setTextColor(230, 230, 230);
                            pdf.setFont("helvetica", "bold");
                            pdf.text("ACHIVOX AI", pageWidth / 2, pageHeight / 2, {
                                align: "center",
                                angle: 45
                            });
                            // Header

                            pdf.setTextColor(79, 70, 229);

                            pdf.setTextColor(148, 163, 184);

                            pdf.setDrawColor(241, 245, 249);
                            pdf.line(15, 12, pageWidth - 15, 12);
                            // Footer

                            pdf.setTextColor(148, 163, 184);

                                align: "right"
                            });
                        }
                    } catch (e) {
                        console.warn("PDF styling skipped:", e);
                    }
                }).outputPdf("blob");
            } finally{
                // Always restore view state
                element.classList.remove("premium-pdf-mode");
                if (pdfSection) pdfSection.classList.add("hidden");
                setIsExporting(false);
            }
            // ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ TIER 1: Capacitor Native Android APK ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
            const isNativeCapacitor =  true && typeof window.Capacitor !== "undefined" && ((_window_Capacitor = window.Capacitor) === null || _window_Capacitor === void 0 ? void 0 : (_window_Capacitor_isNativePlatform = _window_Capacitor.isNativePlatform) === null || _window_Capacitor_isNativePlatform === void 0 ? void 0 : _window_Capacitor_isNativePlatform.call(_window_Capacitor)) === true;
            if (isNativeCapacitor) {

                        url: writeResult.uri,

                } catch (capErr) {

                // Fall through to next tier
                }
            }
            // ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ TIER 2: Android WebView / Mobile browser ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
            // <a download> is blocked in Capacitor WebView; use blob URL + window.open
            const blobUrl = URL.createObjectURL(pdfBlob);
            const isAndroid = typeof navigator !== "undefined" && /android/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
            if (isAndroid) {
                try {

                        setTimeout(()=>URL.revokeObjectURL(blobUrl), 60000);
                        return;
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    console.warn("window.open failed:", e);
                }
            }
            // ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ TIER 3: Standard web browser download ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
